***watervrees.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:watervrees.html>watervrees</a> (58594)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">water</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">water</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrees.html>vrees</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The sense “rabies” <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> from the sore throat caused by the disease, which <a href = vnd.unilang:led.html>led</a> rabids to avoid drinking.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:watervrees.html>watervrees</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hydrophobia, aquaphobia, fear of water
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">aquafobie</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">hydrofobie</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rabies <span class="defdate">[17th-mid 19th c.]</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dolheid.html>dolheid</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hondsdolheid.html>hondsdolheid</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:vrees.html>vrees</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> water</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:angst.html>angst</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drinken.html>drinken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slikken.html>slikken</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:bv.html>bv</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hondsdolheid.html>hondsdolheid</a>.</li></ol>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wagen.html>wage</a></span>, wages</li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wedde.html>wedde</a></strong>

***wedden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wedden.html>wedden</a> (2254)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wedden.html>wedden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*weddon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*weddōn</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*wadjōn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wadjōną</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:wedden.html>wedden</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">wedzje</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:wetten.html>wetten</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wed.html>wed</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">vædde</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">veðja</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wedden.html>wedden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wager, to bet, to accept a gamble
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mag.html>mag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nooit.html>nooit</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wedden.html>wedden</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veroorloven.html>veroorloven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verliezen.html>verliezen</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>You should never bet for more than you can afford to lose.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

***wedstrijd.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wedstrijd.html>wedstrijd</a> (1023)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wed.html>wed</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:strijd.html>strijd</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fight</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, as a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Wettstreit</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">competition</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The German word <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> never <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> common in the sense of an organised match or contest, however. This sense, therefore, must have developed in Dutch either independently or as a calque of another German word, namely <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Wettkampf</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wedstrijd.html>wedstrijd</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wedstrijden.html>wedstrijden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wedstrijdje.html>wedstrijdje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weeg.html>weeg</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wegen.html>wegen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weeg.html>weegje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a wall consisting of a structure of laths and beams with in-between a plaiting of wicker, twigs or straw, filled and flattened with <a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a> or lime</li>
<li>plaited fence</li>
<li>any non-stone wall</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The word occurs as both feminine as masculine and <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> done so as far back as attested.
</p>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">week</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">soft</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dier.html>dier</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">animal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
<ol><li>A mollusc, invertebrate animal of the phylum Mollusca.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">weemoede</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">deep sadness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, backformation from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">weemoedich</i>. The semantic development <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Wehmut</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">wēmōt</i>. <p>Contracted form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weder.html>weder</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">again</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
<ol><li>again
<ul><li><b>1888</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Willem_Kloos" class="extiw" title="w:Willem Kloos"><a href = vnd.unilang:willem.html>Willem</a> Kloos</a>, “O, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haten.html>haten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vergeten.html>vergeten</a>!”
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl">In <a href = vnd.unilang:dreigend.html>dreigend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gillen.html>gillen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> 'k <b>weêr</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:opgestaan.html>opgestaan</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Yelling threateningly I <a href = vnd.unilang:rose.html>rose</a> again.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:weder.html>weder</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">withar</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wether, ram</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*weþruz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wether</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wet-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">year</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weren.html>weren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weertje.html>weertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_8">Etymology 8</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*weraz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:vir.html>vir</a></i>.
</p>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">again</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">already</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weeral.html>weeral</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (once) again

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wederlicht</i>, a form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wederlijc</i> modified by folk etymology. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Wetterleuchten</i>.
